function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/500_resources/hyperlink.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/500_resources/hyperlink.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/500_resources/hyperlink.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/500_resources/hyperlink.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();

	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/500_resources/hyperlink.png');

	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/500_resources/hyperlink.png');
}

	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/500_resources/icon_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/500_resources/icon_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/500_resources/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/500_resources/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}

	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/500_resources/icon_big.png');

	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/500_resources/icon_big.png');
}

if (is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') && (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != 'ae41cca086d56919604980ba750b263720689c47')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_14();
if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');

	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
}

@unlink('plugins/publicPages/501_links/icon_folder_big.png');
if (is_file('plugins/publicPages/501_links/icon_folder_big.png')) {
	warn('File could not be deleted: plugins/publicPages/501_links/icon_folder_big.png');
}

// Dir deleted: plugins/publicPages/501_links
@rmdir('plugins/publicPages/501_links');
if (is_dir('plugins/publicPages/501_links')) {
	warn('Directory could not be deleted (was not empty?): plugins/publicPages/501_links');
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 146\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 146') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');
